When it comes to scientific and physical chemistry books, the science departments of various universities have already gone down the wrong path. The government officials also do not pay attention to it. What I hope for from the major newspapers is to publish more articles about science, which may be of some small help?

The Middle School Student's Predicament 177

— Qian

One day I met a relative who had just graduated from middle school.

I said, "Your three years of high school work have now come to an end. Congratulations."

He frowned and sighed. "Alas, what's there to congratulate? Now I'm going through a difficult time. I'm really disheartened."

I said, "What's making you so unhappy?" He shook his head and said, "When I hadn't graduated yet, I was always thinking about which university to apply to. I thought about going to Peiping. There are good schools there, but it's too far from home. The round-trip fare is really a lot. I thought about studying in Shanghai, but the cost of living is too expensive, and there are limited good schools. After thinking it over, I thought it would be best to apply to Zhongda, because I heard that the equipment inside is very good, and the fees are not high, and it's close to home. So I was always thinking about how to apply to Zhongda. Alas, brother, things are really making me too disheartened. I just received the admissions brochure, and the next day I saw in the newspaper that Zhongda had been dissolved. I was so anxious. I went to ask the teachers, and the teachers said, 'This is just a temporary phenomenon. It will definitely be restored soon.' They told me to prepare as usual. Alas, who knew that the restoration was not only unscheduled, but that they wouldn't even be recruiting this year. What do you think I should do?"

I said, "If they really don't recruit this year, then find something to do and take the exam next year. Isn't that the same?"

He said, "Alas, brother, you're wrong. Where do you think an ordinary middle school student like me can find a job? There are more and more unemployed people every day. People with my qualifications are really a dime a dozen. There's no place to put them. Where can I find a job? As for going to 'Family University,' not only would I be ashamed of being idle, but my youth would be gone, and there would be no opportunity to study in the future. We're really stuck between a rock and a hard place. Like a dumb person eating Coptis chinensis (Chineses goldthread), we can't express our suffering. Only we know it in our hearts. Sigh, it's not just me. There are so many middle school students who have the same plans as me. They're just as miserable as I am."

He was very indignant. He continued, "Sometimes I can't help but hate the government for being irresponsible. Usually, a bunch of bureaucratic politicians like to run education without even investigating it. Once something goes wrong, they just 'dissolve,' 'suspend,' 'seal,' or 'cancel' things, without considering the students' time and studies at all. You want to reorganize, then reorganize. It's easy to restore things in a short amount of time. Who knew it would turn out like this? Where is the government thinking about the students? Where are they treating education as education? If they really treated education as education, things wouldn't have gotten this bad."

Worth Introducing Domestic Goods Factories (9) 178

— He Gongxing

(Fifteen) Fountain Pen Factories

Fountain pens have always come from overseas, especially from Japan, because of their low prices and ability to sell well for a while. In the past four or five years, the Guan Leming Fountain Pen Factory and the Dachina Fountain Pen Factory in Shanghai, one on Kangtuo Road and one in Shencheng Lane on West Axham Road, have been opened by Chinese people.

When manufacturing fountain pens, first make the pen barrel. Most high-quality barrels are made of rubber and rosin. Take the barrel and measure its length, turn the inner and outer screws, and then assemble the upper and lower copper parts, install the water absorption belt, the nib, etc. The copper parts are mostly not self-made, but bought from copper parts makers. This kind of manufacturing by division of labor can reduce costs. As for the nibs, they are entirely foreign goods.

The working machines are small lathe beds, silver hole machines, vices, and several polishing machines. Lathe beds are needed more, so most use motor tows. It is convenient to hold various turning tools in one hand. The important work is also here. Because if the screws on the small pen barrel are not close, the ink will inevitably drip, which will be annoying. Each lathe bed can only produce two or three pens a day, because precise work cannot be done quickly. The market price is eight yuan for each expensive one and around four yuan for cheap ones. Guan Leming can produce one hundred pens per month, and Dachina is similar.

In fact, although the manufacturing process of fountain pens is complicated, in the home, you can start working with a lathe, a hand-cranked small drilling machine, and a small vise. If you produce twenty or thirty pens a month, you can get a family's livelihood.

(Sixteen) Ink Factories

There are six or seven ink manufacturers in Shanghai, including Guan Leming, Minsheng, Dahua, Zhongyi, Jincheng, and China Commercial.

In recent years, fountain pens have become popular among people in the education field, each with a pen, and the ink required for fountain pens has also sold widely. The best ink must be free of impurities, bright in color, and smooth in writing. There are two colors, red and blue, but blue ink is most widely used for pens. The market price of high-quality ink is about two yuan per dozen. The value of foreign goods is more expensive. Most of those who sell in China are overseas Chinese and foreign merchants. Chinese people mostly use domestic goods. Especially people in the education field.

Ink raw materials, such as gallnut color, etc., are mixed with water and refined one or two times to precipitate the impurities. Some add spices to make the smell fragrant, hoping to win the welcome of buyers. Although it is a small thing, the annual sales are also tens of thousands of dollars. Fortunately, manufacturers do not need much equipment and do not need labor. Thirty to fifty dollars can be used to manufacture it at home. The decoration is also extremely simple.

Most of the ink manufacturers also produce ink for writing brushes. The raw material is ink powder. At first, the manufacturers all used the pine soot ink powder from the old days in China. Later, they used the ink powder used for manufacturing printing ink for foreign goods, which was more suitable, and mostly changed to use it, because it has no impurities and the concentration is uniform. It is a pity that the cost is more expensive. All other manufacturing procedures are the same as ink.

Brief News: Recently, a well-known veteran of the art world has established a new literary and art club on Luban Road, specializing in the sale of ancient and modern calligraphy and paintings. He is now collecting hundreds of fan surfaces of calligraphy and paintings by famous modern figures from the north and south, and plans to open a fan surface exhibition within the month. Among them, there are many that are not easy to obtain, such as Mr. Qin Zizhi, who is eighty years old this year, and the fan surface he wrote is still full of energy. Sun Chengshimin, the grandson of the "ten-hair old man," is only twelve years old. His landscape paintings directly emulate the works of famous figures in the Three Dingjia. There are also many works by the top scholar Liu Runqin, who has long withdrawn the fee for his paintings, and cannot be sought except by those he knows. There are also many works by famous artists such as Ye Guangquan, Cheng Ten Hair, Kuang You, and Han. The beautiful and incomparable sights cannot be taken in all at once.

Record of Striking the Bell at an Ancient Temple (54) 179

—斋夫 Who Does Not Weed the Courtyard

Sixty-one

Mr. Zhu's argument is like quinine; the first taste is sweet, but as soon as you mistakenly bite down, you immediately taste the bitterness. He always adds one or two pieces of bitter melon under the candy, making it hard for you to swallow. For example, when he hears about the so-called six major trainings, the first five are undoubtedly good. Why add this reproductive training? (Good birth) is certainly something everyone agrees with. Who would want to give birth to bad children? (Giving birth to a dragon or a snake all depends on the old man in the sky.) Although this is a superstitious saying, it makes sense if you regard this old man in the sky as the old man of nature. Who can say for sure that he will give birth to good children and not bad children? From the ordinary point of view, the children of Emperor Yao should all be good, but why did he give birth to a degenerate Danzhu? On the other hand, it is not surprising that 瞽叟 gave birth to an arrogant Xiang, but why did he also give birth to a supremely filial and wise Shun? Can Mr. Zhu teach Yao not to give birth to Danzhu? Can he teach 瞽叟 not to give birth to Xiang but only to Shun? As for the three words (bear fewer), I understand them even less. Now that China is oppressed by imperialism, it should encourage reproduction and use the power of its large population to resist. How can it teach people to have fewer children to reduce national power? Moreover, Mr. Zhu often says that recruiting students is like Han Xin counting soldiers, the more the better, but now he wants to advocate reducing the population, which is really beyond my expectation. To be honest, I can't swallow this piece of bitter melon. I dare not blindly follow, but I don't want to criticize thoughtlessly. At the same time, I admit that Mr. Zhu is not just talking nonsense. He must have some facts as the basis for his argument. I want to examine the facts he is based on before criticizing his argument, and finally decide whether I agree with this argument. After I made up my mind, I said to Mr. Zhu: (I am very skeptical about your claim to reduce the population, and now I want to ask you to give me some factual evidence.) Mr. Zhu said: Your attitude is a fundamental attitude for scholars to do scholarship (bring evidence!) Academic theory must be based on evidence to be indestructible. However, I have further hope for you. Since you doubt my argument, you will inevitably doubt the facts I have collected. I hope you will take two steps as one, and collect facts on the population problem yourself, so that these facts will naturally elicit arguments. Don't have a trace of prejudice in your heart. When you filter out arguments from the facts, compare them with my facts and arguments to see whose is right. At that time, if mine is right, you will abandon your argument; if yours is right, I will definitely abandon my argument and follow you. If you have the opportunity to go to the city, you can go to the university library, the municipal library, and other libraries to browse the works on population issues, and then run to the source of facts in society to conduct detailed interviews yourself. This work is very interesting. You can do it at your leisure. Fortunately, my one-copper-coin birth control method has not yet been invented, and it is not too late to decide our policy after you have studied it.) Okay, let's do it that way.

Red Bar Balance Not Thin

The bidding gold situation last week, although there were no special changes, formed a pattern of circling. The situation was elusive, and the price turned upward day by day, at most seven or eight taels. The intentions of colleagues were uncertain, so the demand and supply were different. On Tuesday, it showed a profit, probably because the exchange market seemed tight. It once rose to 53 taels and 7 mace. Later, the exchange rate rose continuously. Estimated Small One Yuan to Two Yuan Seven or Eight Jiao

The market transaction situation of the Chinese Merchants Securities Exchange last week (from July 18 to 23), with few spot goods coming in and out, and even more desolate in the last few days of the week. It is estimated that only 41,000 yuan were opened for the whole week, of which 11,000 yuan was for the 19th Customs, 8,000 yuan for salt tax, 6,000 yuan for finance, and only a few thousand yuan for the rest. Shen Bao Local Supplement

Words

Truly Beyond Cure 189

— Buddha

Only with a good society can there be a good government, and only with good citizens can there be good leaders. When I examine our country's society and the nature of its people, I am filled with pessimism everywhere. The words "truly beyond cure" can encompass it all. There are many such events, and I will try to list three examples below:

Young people are especially prone to suicide. Suicide due to failed romance, suicide due to academic failure, suicide due to economic oppression. This kind of suicidal behavior completely demonstrates a lack of fighting spirit and strong character. As soon as they encounter setbacks, they think of ending their lives. This kind of concept completely reveals the fragility of the national character and the lack of the ability to shoulder heavy responsibilities and go the distance. This is the first instance of what I call "beyond cure."

As reported in newspapers, when our countrymen are kidnapped or robbed, foreigners, upon hearing of this, will bravely and selflessly come to their aid. However, our own people, even those who are police officers or patrolmen whose duty it is to maintain law and order, often shrink back when they hear of an alarm, thinking that it is not worth sacrificing their lives for a few tens of dollars in salary. Even within a family, it is likely the same. Fathers and brothers, seeing their sons and younger brothers being kidnapped, are secretly pleased that they themselves escaped. Sons and younger brothers, seeing their fathers and elder brothers being robbed, are secretly pleased that they escaped quickly. As for neighbors being kidnapped or robbed, they are even more likely to close their doors tightly, not daring to go out. This kind of selfish and self-serving mentality is the root cause of national and familial ruin. It is unique to our countrymen, who disregard public morality and do not understand righteousness. Such a group of people will naturally fall apart. This is the second instance of what I call "beyond cure."

The September 18th Incident and the January 28th Incident. The shame and suffering our country has endured were so severe. How long ago was it that the five-minute burst of enthusiasm has already passed? People are now resenting and abandoning each other, completely forgetting the past. According to the customs trade reports, the import of Japanese goods to the South last month decreased by only 15% compared to last year. The import to the North even exceeded last year by 25%. This one point alone is enough to show that the people's hearts are dead. What else is there to say? Moreover, Puyi even took advantage of the incidents to become a puppet, and people in Jiangbei took advantage of the incidents to become traitors. Our countrymen have no conscience and no concept of the nation. It has reached this extreme. This is the third instance of what I call "beyond cure."

The above situations, if you pay attention, can be seen everywhere in our society. These matters seem small, but the country's hopelessness, helplessness, and lack of a way out lie in them.

Social Reform Discussion Society

Discussion on Reforming Men's Clothing with an Additional Suggestion to Reform Women's Shorts 190

The other day, Mr. Zhang Su suggested reforming men's clothing. Indeed, the current clothing needs to be reformed. Not only should men's long robes, which drag in the mud and water, be reformed, but also women's shorts, which are now so short that they expose the thighs, should also be reformed. Otherwise, these two temptations of exposed thighs will mislead countless young people.

Clothes are meant to protect the body. Men's woolen socks in summer and women's silk stockings and shorts in winter are too unhygienic. Speaking of Western suits, although they are beautiful and convenient, wearing them is too troublesome and too aristocratic. Moreover, wearing only shorts in the summer is too stuffy. Therefore, this member suggests that men's clothing should follow the style of student uniforms for the upper body, which is both convenient and elegant, and conforms to Mr. Zhang's principle of "no longer than the knees and no shorter than the waist." It can also express the attitude of a scholar. As for the lower body, I think shorts are the most lightweight and suitable, but the length should reach the knees, otherwise it would be indecent.

An old villager saw the modern young masters and ladies and raised a question, saying that it can truly be considered civilization now. Women's pants have gone from very long to now seemingly nonexistent. Men, on the other hand, have gone from shorts (many farmers wear shorts) to pants that almost drag on the ground. Alas, strange, is it civilization? Or demonization? Therefore, this member wants to attach a suggestion to reform women's shorts in addition to discussing men's clothing.

Reasons:

(1) Short pants and thin silk stockings cannot protect the body in cold weather.

(2) They are detrimental to public morals and tempt young people to go astray. Therefore, this member proposes that the length of women's pants must be longer than the knees. Is this appropriate? Please submit it to your association for joint discussion by all members. Respectfully, Social Reform Discussion Society. Member: Huai Jingcheng

Suggestions for Reforming the Marriage System 191

— Zhang Dingming

In this era of the intersection of new and old ideas, before all the old systems of our Chinese society are thoroughly destroyed and new revolutionary buildings are rebuilt, all phenomena in society are distorted. In particular, the most important issue in the surging history of life is marriage. This issue has a significant relationship with society and will also affect the future of the country and the nation. Because the family is the foundation of society, and the family is based on marriage as a prerequisite, so we must study national issues and social reform. In addition to the new construction of education and politics, I dare say this is also an important issue. Looking at recent times, aren't people committing suicide enthusiastically for marriage? If we let it grow without taking measures, wouldn't there be great harm to society! I can first talk about the evils of the old marriage system in general:

1. The union of old marriages is completely dictated by the old ethics: "Parents' orders and matchmakers' words." Neither party can meet, nor can they mutually examine each other's character, family situation, and everything else. Everything is based on false material goals. Such blind marriages cannot be established on the principle of love at all. You must know that marriage should be based on love, otherwise it will only result in a resentful couple, and they will feel immense pain and sorrow in their spirits for the rest of their lives.

2. The procedures for old marriages are both troublesome, and all the rituals are too feudal and wasteful under this revolutionary trend. Like bride price (which can be said to be a sale of one's body), and the arguing over the length of clothing and decorations, and the ostentatious display of face, the marriage expenses of those in the bourgeoisie often consume thousands or tens of thousands of yuan. Those in the petty bourgeoisie even go bankrupt or incur heavy debts because of it, while those in the proletariat simply cannot talk about it. They can only embrace celibacy invisibly. Many young people with true love cannot achieve a satisfactory ending due to the encirclement of this evil custom, or even lead to tragedy. Therefore, this man-eating old custom must be thoroughly eliminated, and at the same time, the government should strictly prohibit it. If there are those who outwardly comply but inwardly defy, and do not obey the prohibition, they must be given appropriate punishment.

3. There is no standard for the age limit for old marriages. There are underage and immature men and women who are forced by their parents to marry early, which damages their physical strength and life expectancy. In the affairs of the country and society, they are also indirectly harmed. This should also be strictly prohibited by the government.

In addition to striving to overthrow the above-mentioned obstacles to sacred love, we must also do the following:

1. The end point of love is marriage. Marriage is an urgent pursuit in our life history. If there is no deep understanding and careful consideration beforehand, it will inevitably lead to lifelong regret and an indelible trauma, leading to a decline in will, or even a lack of interest in the world. Therefore, after we get to know each other, we must have an understanding of the following conditions before we can enter into an engagement: A. Understanding of each other's character. B. Examination of academic level. C. Testing the truth of the love. D. Investigation of family situation. In short, the standard of marriage in this era should not be mixed with material things or sexual pursuits and other influential conditions. After doing it this way, there will definitely be painful results. In this distorted society, among hypocritical humans, we should rather be prudent at the beginning, and not leave regret for later.

2. When both parties in the above first article are satisfied, and there has been a considerable period of love, an introducer can be invited to obtain the consent of both parents, and then enter into an engagement. The method should be the simplest, absolutely abolishing the buying and selling style. The method is as follows: Both parties exchange tokens of love, take commemorative engagement photos together, or announce it in the newspaper.

3. After the engagement, when there is a possibility of bearing family burdens in one's own productive capacity, one can get married. The ceremony should be based on the newest style ceremony as the standard. In fact, absolutely no extravagance should be made, and no money should be wasted. For example, hold the ceremony in a hotel or in the auditorium of any organization or group. Relatives and friends who attend the wedding should be prepared with tea and snacks or simple wine and dishes to show joy. To the simplest, this kind of formal etiquette is not necessary. As long as both parties agree, they can announce in the newspaper and start living together. Love focuses on the spirit, so there is no need to stick to the form.

Literary Arts

I Have Worn the Same Clothes and Hat for Three Years; Recently, It Has Been Very Hot, and a Friend Advised Me to Change My Clothes for the Season. I Wrote This to Thank Him. 192

— Chen Wangzun

How can one be so cold?

Even in summer, I wear winter clothes.

The blackness does not reach the ink stand,

How can heat enter the rustic spleen?

I often have the intention of approaching the abyss,

It is not without thoughts of correcting the world.

How many cold and hot seasons in life?

How much heat can one get?

Entrusting my body to a coffin,

That is my summer escape.

Song of Bitter Heat 193

—

The heat is very intense,

Not entering the houses of the rich,

Only scorching the backs of rickshaw pullers,

Burning a piece of their flesh.

Burning them until they are about to ignite,

They run quickly, but still not fast enough.

The young rickshaw pullers shake their straw hats,

Gazing at the tall buildings with envious eyes.

Hurriedly dragging to the alley entrance,

They argue over a few copper coins.

Alas, you must not argue over what is not enough,

Idle rickshaw pullers by the roadside,

Their backs are scorched, and they are hungry and crying.

Science

How to Make White Pigments 194

— Ming

There are many types of white pigments, among which the most important are the following four. Now I will describe their manufacturing methods separately:

(1) Basic Carbonate White Lead (PbCO3)2Pb(OH)2: This pigment is made by the interaction of carbon dioxide and lead oxide. There are two methods:

(1) French Method: Dissolve lead oxide as much as possible in an aqueous solution of lead acetate to make basic lead acetate. Then, carbon dioxide is introduced, and white lead powder precipitates out. Filter it, and the filtrate still contains lead acetate, so lead oxide can be dissolved again to make white lead powder. This is the new method.

(2) Dutch Method: Put acetic acid (the strength of which is about the same as acid vinegar) in earthen bottles, place lead plates on top, and surround them with waste animal and plant matter. Because of its fermentation, heat and carbon dioxide are released. Acetic acid forms vapor due to heat and interacts with lead to produce basic lead acetate, which is then transformed into basic carbonate lead salt, that is, basic carbonate white lead powder, under the action of carbon dioxide. These reactions are very slow, taking about 100 to 130 days. This is the old method.

The percentage composition of basic carbonate white lead powder is approximately 75% lead carbonate and 25% lead hydroxide, or 85% lead hydroxide and 15% carbon dioxide and water. When it comes into contact with hydrogen sulfide gas, it turns black because black lead sulfide is produced.

(2) Zinc White (ZnO): There are two methods for its preparation:

(1) American Method: Use anthracite to reduce zinc ore to metallic zinc. Its vapor flows out from the top of the furnace, mixes with air, and burns into zinc white.

(2) French Method: Refine metallic zinc in flowing air, generating vapor, which burns into zinc oxide (i.e., pure white) white fumes.

Zinc white is bright and pure white, and is mostly used for porcelain glaze. It does not change color when it reacts with sulfide gas, because zinc sulfide is also white.

(3) Basic Sulfate White Lead (PbSO4)2Pb(OH)2: Bake galena (PbS), and the fumes that are volatilized are oxidized in the air to form basic sulfate white lead powder. This is a very good white pigment. Its percentage composition is 75% lead sulfate, 20% lead oxide, and 5% zinc oxide. Its chemical properties are extremely stable, and it will not turn black when reacting with sulfides. It is better than basic carbonate white lead powder for coating wooden objects.

(4) Lithopone (BaSO4ZnS): The method of manufacturing this pigment is to mix solutions of zinc sulfate and barium sulfide, which will precipitate insoluble barium sulfate and zinc sulfide at the same time. The reaction is:

ZnSO4 + BaS → ZnS + BaSO4

This precipitate contains 70% to 75% barium sulfate, and the rest is zinc sulfide. This mixed precipitate is not suitable for use as a pigment. It must be calcined to a dark red color and suddenly thrown into water to form soft blocks. Then, it is ground into powder, washed with water, and dried to become a very good white pigment.

A Corner of Society

Going to Listen to Storytelling 195

— Yi Ping

Of course, going to listen to storytelling is not as fashionable as playing golf, but from a certain standpoint, the storytelling venue still has no shortage of listeners. In Shanghai, wherever you can find a rectangular wooden board hanging above a fried bun stall, it is written that "This building has specially invited Guangyu Society's famous artist XXX to perform XXX", etc. You university students in wide-leg pants and young masters in stiff collars must not recklessly step up this shaky staircase, because when you see the few square feet of this humble room, with several benches lying haphazardly, the ground covered with melon seed shells, and the unique smell, you will shake your head and quickly turn back the last step that has not yet stepped on the floor.

What is now being said about "going to listen to storytelling" obviously does not refer to listening to the Shanghai opera tune. Like a few old seniors, bending over and arching their water pipes, are nailed to the fixed seat (slang) regardless of wind and rain, like smoking opium, they cannot live a day without it. You must first dress yourself in a flowery attire. The Western-style pants must be ironed like the vertical lines in geometry, and the two-inch high stiff collar supports your entire head. After dinner, wander around on Nanjing Road. Two sharp eyes seek your starting point, and send yourself into the body from the towering room, lying in a comfortable armchair, drinking delicious fragrant tea, not asking who is singing on the stage, your ears can steal listening to the private whispers in the next seat, and if there is a chance to interject, like a golden fly stinging a stinky duck egg, you can add to it. If you are a politician-style socialite, it is not difficult to get the other party's response, because their slogan is, "Everyone here is our comrade," and a comrade of course has the right to speak. Your eyes are even more free, as you look around left and right, and your nose also uses its wonders. Under the gentle electric fan, you can no longer think of those proletarians who are sleeping unsteadily because the heat in the house is too high, lying on the asphalt road and being coveted by city tigers. If really all of this does not suit your taste, you can close your eyelids and go to the dreamland to pursue everything you want. The price of twenty cents will not be considered a great loss in your life.

Empty Words

Poor Ah K 196

— Wang Ying

Ah K, the eldest sister in the Huang Mansion, is so lovely. Every part of her demeanor shows her health and beauty. Her jet-black hair, oval face, full breasts, and vigorous steps – she really doesn't look like someone who works as an eldest sister.

Meisheng, the young master in the Huang Mansion, is a young man who calls himself a romantic talent. When he saw how beautiful Ah K had grown, he immediately had bad intentions. He did not hesitate to use his position as a young master to mess around with her. As for Ah K? After all, she doesn't understand the ways of the world. In her eyes, she thought that getting the young master's favor was the supreme glory. She couldn't resist Meisheng's sweet words and various temptations, and she finally became intoxicated and lost her chastity.

Unexpectedly, their secret was discovered by Meisheng's mother. The old lady thought that the relationship between master and servant was a great shame. She couldn't help but give Meisheng a lesson first, and then suspended Ah K, while scolding her ("rotten goods, shameless thing"). Poor Ah K, although she was harboring endless resentment, she did not dare to resist at all, and she had no courage to tell Mrs. Huang that Meisheng had already destroyed her chastity. All that could be seen was her head down, tears flowing, slowly walking out of the Huang family's door.

Jiangsu High Court Second Branch 198

▲Criminal Judgment▲One case of Ding Wu's opium case (main text) appeal dismissed▲Ruling one case of Pan Ruifu's lawsuit against Zhu Yongsheng for embezzlement (main text) application rejected▲One case of Yu Weiwen's private prosecution of Lu Lanchun, that is, Xue Yu's abandonment case (main text) the original ruling is revoked

▲Criminal Judgment▲One case of Liu Gu's cannon, etc. for robbery (main text) the original judgment on the part of Liu Gu's cannon, Chen Youlin is revoked. Liu Gu's cannon is a repeat offender who jointly robbed Chen Gongliang and is sentenced to ten years of imprisonment. As a repeat offender, he jointly robbed Lian Qitai, Shi Yuanbin, and Li Zhiqing of three crimes and is sentenced to fourteen years of imprisonment for each crime. The term of imprisonment should be fourteen years. Chen Youlin is sentenced to seven years of imprisonment for each of the two crimes of jointly committing robbery. The term of imprisonment should be seven years. The number of days of detention before the judgment is determined shall be offset by one day of imprisonment for every two days. ▲One case of Gu Wensheng and Chen Zhongci, etc. because the defendant, etc. appealed the case of theft and obstructing freedom (main text) the appeal is dismissed▲One case of Ye Guisheng and Tang Santai, etc. because the self-accused defendant, etc. appealed the case of false accusation (main text) the appeal is dismissed

▲Civil Judgment▲One case of Hu Ziyu and Feng Haifu's litigation over advance money (main text) The original judgment is changed. Feng Haifu shall repay Hu Liao Yu silver six thousand three hundred and forty-six taels, two maces, one cent and seven mills, and five percent interest per annum from July 1, the twentieth year of the Republic of China until the date of repayment. Feng Haifu's appeal is dismissed. The first and second trial costs shall be borne by Feng Haifu (above July 23)

Shanghai First Special District Local Court 199

▲Civil Judgment: Ni Runxiang vs. Shen A'da Debt Case: Defendant Kui Maokang should repay the plaintiff 135 yuan in silver dollars; the plaintiff's remaining claims are dismissed; court costs are to be borne one-half by the defendant and one-half by the plaintiff.

▲Texaco Company's Newlon vs. Lanxing Company shareholder Xu Xianghua et al. for Goods: The defendants, et al., should jointly and severally repay the plaintiff 633 yuan, 2 jiao, and 1 fen, with annual interest of 5% from the date of the lawsuit until the date of execution; court costs are to be borne jointly and severally by the defendants, et al.

▲Ge Tasheng vs. Tong Fuhai et al. Loan Case: The defendants should jointly and severally repay the plaintiff 60 yuan in silver dollars; court costs are to be borne jointly and severally by the defendants, et al.

▲Xin Gengxiang vs. Shao Wenmei Debt Case: The plaintiff's claim is dismissed; court costs are to be borne by the plaintiff.

▲Xu Wenbin vs. Chuan Ruiquan Debt Case: The defendant should repay the plaintiff 621 taels and 5 qian in silver, with interest calculated monthly at 1% from June 1, 1930, until the date of repayment; court costs are to be borne by the defendant.

▲Ge Jinxing vs. Shen Zhuchen et al. Debt Case: The defendant Shen Zhuchen should repay the plaintiff 1,000 yuan in silver dollars; if he is unable to repay, the defendant Bao Zhenyao shall repay on his behalf; court costs are to be borne by the defendant Shen Zhuchen.

▲Zhe Bisheng vs. Yang A'gen et al. Loan Case: The defendant Yang A'gen should repay the plaintiff 800 yuan in silver dollars; this amount is to be repaid at a rate of 10 yuan per month until the debt is cleared; if he is unable to repay, the defendant Lu Jinrong shall be responsible for repaying on his behalf; court costs are to be borne by the defendant Yang A'gen.

▲China Reclamation Bank Real Estate Department Li Hanchu vs. Tang Hangjian Promissory Note Case: The defendant should repay the plaintiff 350 yuan in silver dollars; court costs are to be borne by the defendant.

▲Dai Xin vs. Dadong Automotive Oil Company Gong Yuanlang et al. Security Deposit Case: The defendant should repay the plaintiff 118 yuan in silver dollars; the plaintiff's remaining claims and application for provisional execution are dismissed; court costs are to be borne two-thirds by the defendant and one-third by the plaintiff.

▲Weng Ke'an vs. Du Yougen Account Case: The defendant should repay the plaintiff 302 taels and 5 qian and 2 fen of standard silver and also 141 yuan and 6 jiao and 4 fen in silver dollars; court costs are to be borne by the defendant.

▲Fei Erkesi vs. Lao Rensiji Promissory Note Case: The plaintiff's claim is dismissed; court costs are to be borne by the plaintiff.

▲He Fengzhuang vs. Xian Chang Kun Kee Woolen Goods Store Manager Hu Mingshu Debt Case: The defendant should repay the plaintiff 4,408 taels of silver, with agreed-upon interest calculated at 5 taels per thousand taels per month from the date of the lawsuit until the date of execution; court costs are to be borne by the defendant.

▲Qiu Yaogen vs. Zhang Zhaochun Debt, etc. Case: The defendant should vacate the house within one month from the date of the judgment; the plaintiff's remaining claims are dismissed; court costs are to be borne half by each party; if the defendant does not vacate by the deadline and the case is not yet final, provisional execution shall be granted.

▲Bo Gesheng vs. Zhang A'ru et al. Loan Case: The defendant Zhang A'ru should repay the plaintiff 200 yuan in silver dollars; this amount is to be repaid at a rate of 20 yuan per month until the debt is cleared; if he is unable to repay, the defendant Yang Qifa shall repay on his behalf; court costs are to be borne by the defendant.

▲Lu Ke vs. Wu Xianghua Rent Arrears Case: The defendant should pay the plaintiff, the manager of Tonghe Company, 620 yuan in rent; the plaintiff's remaining claims are dismissed; court costs are to be borne one-fifth by the plaintiff and four-fifths by the defendant; the plaintiff's application for provisional execution is dismissed.

▲Guo Yangmo et al. vs. Shen Zhaotong et al. Compensation Case: The plaintiff's claim is dismissed; court costs are to be borne by the plaintiff.

▲Chen Boqing vs. Zheng Jinshui et al. Goods Price Case: The defendant Zheng Jinshui should pay the plaintiff 695 silver dollars, with annual interest calculated at 5% from May 21, 1932, until the date of payment; if Zheng Jinshui does not pay, Cheng Peixi shall be responsible for paying on his behalf; the plaintiff's remaining claims are dismissed; court costs are to be borne two-thirds by the plaintiff and one-third by the defendant.

▲Li Mulian vs. Zhu Baoyuan Contract Confirmation Case: Confirmation that the settlement acknowledged by both parties has the effect that both parties should perform in accordance with the settlement; court costs are to be borne by the defendant.

▲Xu Yongqing vs. Wei Fengxiang Debt Case: The defendant should repay the plaintiff 242 taels and 5 qian in silver, with annual interest of 5% from January 15, 1932, until the date of execution; court costs, excluding the application fee which is to be borne by the plaintiff, are to be borne by the defendant; the plaintiff's application for provisional execution is dismissed.

▲Mu Su vs. Kaitai Firm Owner Xue Yi Rent Arrears Case: The defendant should repay the plaintiff 70 taels of silver; court costs relating to the defendant's part of the claim are to be borne by the defendant.

▲Xincheng Timber Firm Zhang Jinrong vs. Tang Yueting Rent Arrears Case: The defendant should repay the plaintiff 360 yuan in silver dollars and vacate the house; court costs are to be borne by the defendant.

▲Shen Yongyao vs. Zhou Changda Rent Arrears Case: The defendant should repay the plaintiff 690 yuan in rent and acknowledges that the plaintiff has a lien on the defendant's belongings left in the house; court costs are to be borne by the defendant.

▲Chen Huisheng vs. Jiang Yunlaoliu et al. Rent Arrears Case: The defendants Jiang Yunlaoliu, Zhu Xushi, Zhou A'si, and Teng Ronggen should each repay the plaintiff 900 yuan in silver dollars; the defendant Xu Qidong should repay the plaintiff 580 yuan in silver dollars; court costs are to be borne by the defendants proportionally.

▲Siwen Foreign Firm Kaobumen vs. Tang Yunlong Rent Arrears Case: The defendant should repay the plaintiff 558 yuan in rent and return the house; court costs are to be borne by the defendant; provisional execution shall be granted in respect of the part of the case relating to vacating the premises.

▲Taili Company Lessee Tao Wenbin vs. Cheng Changling Rent Arrears Case: The defendant should repay the plaintiff 120 yuan in rent; court costs are to be borne by the defendant.

▲Chen Jisheng vs. Pan A'shun Rent Arrears Case: The defendant should repay the plaintiff 66 yuan in silver dollars; the plaintiff's remaining claims are dismissed; court costs are to be borne by the defendant and the other defendants sentenced in this case proportionally.

▲Xu Huangqing vs. Wang Bingyan Rent Arrears Case: The defendant should repay the plaintiff 78 yuan in silver dollars; court costs are to be borne by the defendant and the other defendants sentenced in this case proportionally.

▲Pu Xinxin vs. Shao A'xiang et al. Loan Case: The defendant Shao A'xiang should repay the plaintiff 100 yuan in silver dollars; if he is unable to repay, the defendants Wang Maodou and Yu Yicheng shall jointly and severally repay on his behalf; court costs are to be borne by Shao A'xiang.

▲A'desheng vs. Wang Shoushan et al. Debt Case: The defendant Wang Shoushan should repay the plaintiff 300 yuan in silver dollars; if he is unable to repay, the defendant Zhang Jinsheng shall repay on his behalf; court costs are to be borne by the defendant Wang Shoushan.

▲Lun Sheng vs. Zhang Deyuan et al. Debt Case: The defendants Zhang Deyuan, Gao Fei, and Zhu Wanqing should jointly and severally repay the plaintiff 350 yuan in silver dollars; the defendants Zhang Deyuan, Chen Defang, and Feng Langzhai should jointly and severally repay the plaintiff 180 yuan in silver dollars; court costs are to be borne by the defendants jointly and severally in proportion to the amount of their respective claims.

▲Wang Shaoshan vs. Zhu Jinfan et al. Debt Case: The defendant Zhu Jinfan should repay the plaintiff 375 yuan in silver dollars; the defendant Ying Anqing should repay the plaintiff 100 yuan in silver dollars, with interest calculated at 1.2% per month from the date of their respective loans until the date of execution; if he is unable to repay, the defendant Zhu Jinfan shall repay on his behalf; court costs are to be borne by the defendants in proportion to the amount of their respective claims.

▲Suilongsheng Rice Shop Yao Wenxiang vs. Shunxing Restaurant Owner Hu Xiaogeng Debt Case: The defendant should repay the plaintiff 266 yuan and 2 jiao in silver dollars; this amount is to be repaid at a rate of 50 yuan per month until the debt is cleared; court costs, excluding the application fee which is to be borne by the plaintiff, are to be borne by the defendant; the plaintiff's application for provisional execution is dismissed.

▲Anli Company vs. Taikang Printing House Manager Xie Zhijian Rent Arrears Case: The defendant should repay the plaintiff 232 yuan in rent, vacate the house, and acknowledges that the plaintiff has a lien on the defendant's machinery placed in the rented house; the plaintiff's remaining claims are dismissed; court costs are to be borne two-tenths by the plaintiff and eight-tenths by the defendant; provisional execution shall be granted in respect of the part of the case relating to vacating the premises.

▲Chen Qihua vs. Hongkou Grand Hotel et al. Security Deposit Case: The defendant Hongkou Grand Hotel should repay the plaintiff 2,000 yuan in silver dollars and annual interest of 5% from January 15 of this year until the date of execution; the defendants Chen Huanzhi et al. shall be responsible for clearing and repaying the aforementioned debt; the plaintiff's remaining claims are dismissed; court costs are to be borne by the defendant Hongkou Grand Hotel.
